<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;1.01</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>I.</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Introduction</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On December&nbsp;28, 2004, Charles A. Bittenbender, the Vice President, General Counsel and
Secretary of NACCO Industries, Inc. (&#147;NACCO&#148;) and Assistant Secretary of The North American Coal
Corporation (&#147;NA Coal&#148;), the NACCO Materials Handling Group, Inc. (&#147;NMHG&#148;), Hamilton
Beach/Proctor-Silex, Inc. (&#147;HB/PS&#148;) and The Kitchen Collection, Inc. (&#147;KCI&#148;) (NACCO, NA Coal, NMHG,
HB/PS and KCI are referred to collectively as (the &#147;Company&#148;) executed amendments, effective
January&nbsp;1, 2005, to certain benefit arrangements affecting executive officers in response to the
passage of the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004 (the &#147;Jobs Act&#148;). Specifically, Mr.&nbsp;Bittenbender
executed amendments to the following Company benefit arrangements:

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>II.</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>The Amendments to the NACCO Unfunded Plan, the Rankin Plan, the VAP, the NA Coal Deferred
Compensation Plan, the NMHG Unfunded Plan, the HB/PS Unfunded Plan, and the KCI Deferred
Compensation Plan (collectively, the &#147;Deferred Plans&#148;)</B>


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always"><A HREF="#toc">Table of Contents</A></H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The amendments to the Deferred Plans create additional sub-accounts within each such plan to
reflect amounts that are &#147;deferred&#148; as such term is defined in the guidance issued by the Internal
Revenue Service with regard to the Jobs Act (the &#147;Guidance&#148;) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 and earnings
thereon (the &#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148;) and amounts that are deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004
and earnings thereon (the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Accounts&#148;). The Grandfathered Sub-Accounts will remain
subject to the provisions of the plans in effect prior to the enactment of the Jobs Act and the law
applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code,
to the extent permitted by the Jobs Act and the Guidance. The Post-2004 Sub-Accounts will be
subject to the amended plan provisions that implement the restrictions of the Jobs Act. In
addition, each of the plans was amended to allow participants in the plans to make appropriate
deferral elections and to receive distributions under the plans in compliance with the Jobs Act.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The amendments to the NA Coal Deferred Compensation Plan, NMHG Unfunded Plan and the HB/PS
Unfunded Plan revise the claims procedures for each of the plans.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Finally, the amendment to the KCI Deferred Compensation Plan provides that on and after
January&nbsp;1, 2005, participants may only elect to defer LTIP awards that (1)&nbsp;are 100% vested as of
December&nbsp;31, 2004, (2)&nbsp;have grant dates of January&nbsp;1, 2004 and (3)&nbsp;are validly and timely deferred
under the KCI LTIP.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>III.</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>The Amendments to the NMHG LTIP, the NMHG Senior Executive LTIP, the HB/PS LTIP, the HB/PS
Senior Executive LTIP and the KCI LTIP (collectively, the &#147;LTIP Plans&#148;)</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The amendments to the LTIP Plans create two sets of Awards under each such plan &#151; the
&#147;Pre-2005 Awards&#148; for Awards that are &#147;deferred,&#148; as such term is defined in the Guidance, as of
December&nbsp;31, 2004 and the &#147;Post-2004 Awards&#148; for Awards that are deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004.
The Pre-2005 Awards will remain subject to provisions of the plans in effect prior to the enactment
of the Jobs Act and the law applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to the addition
of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, to the extent permitted by the Jobs Act and the Guidance. The
Post-2004 Awards will be subject to the amended plan provisions that implement the restrictions of
the Jobs Act. In addition, each of the plans was amended to allow participants in the plans to
make appropriate deferral elections and to receive distributions under the plans in compliance with
the Jobs Act.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>IV.</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>The SERP and the UK Plan (collectively, the &#147;Frozen Plans&#148;)</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The amendments to the Frozen Plans temporarily freeze benefit accruals under each such plan
with the intent being that the freeze will be rescinded in the future.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, the amendment to the SERP revises the claims procedures for the SERP.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>V.</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Exhibits to Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each of the amendments to the Deferred Plans, LTIP Plans and the Frozen Plans is attached to
this Current Report on From 8-K and is hereby incorporated herein by reference. Each of the
foregoing summaries of the amendments to the Deferred Plans, the LTIP Plans and the Frozen Plans is
qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of such plan attached hereto as an exhibit.

<TYPE>EX-10.1

<FILENAME>l11171aexv10w1.htm
<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #6 NACCO INDUSTRIES UNFUNDED BENEFIT PLAN

<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.1</TITLE>

<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt">Exhibit 10.1

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 6<BR>
TO<BR>
THE NACCO INDUSTRIES, INC.<BR>
UNFUNDED BENEFIT PLAN<BR>
(Effective September&nbsp;1, 2000)<BR>
WITH RESPECT TO<BR>
THE AMERICAN JOBS CREATION ACT OF 2004</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, NACCO Industries, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) adopted the Unfunded
Benefit Plan (the &#147;Plan&#148;) effective as of September&nbsp;1, 2000 and has since
amended the Plan; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to Section&nbsp;6.1 of the Plan, all amounts credited to a
Participant&#146;s Account under the Plan are 100% vested; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, to the fullest extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A and the AJCA
Guidance, the Company wants to protect the &#147;grandfathered&#148; status of the Excess
Retirement Benefits that were deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW THEREFORE, the Company hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;6 to the Plan,
which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 (including any earnings thereon) to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and
continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred
compensation, and the terms of the Plan as in effect, prior to the addition of
Code Section&nbsp;409A and (2)&nbsp;cause amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 to be
deferred in compliance with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words used herein with initial capital letters that are defined in the Plan are
used herein as so defined.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;I of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Section&nbsp;1.5 to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;1.5 American Jobs Creation Act (AJCA).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;It is intended that the Plan (including all Amendments thereto) comply
with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as enacted by AJCA, so as to
prevent the inclusion in gross income of any Excess Retirement Benefit
hereunder in a taxable year that is prior to the taxable year or years in which
such amounts would otherwise actually be distributed or made available to the
Participants. The Plan shall be administered in a manner that will comply with
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, including any proposed,


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">temporary or final regulations or any other guidance issued by the Secretary of
the Treasury and the Internal Revenue Service with respect thereto
(collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;). Any Plan provisions
(including, without limitation, those added or amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;6) that
would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A of the Code shall have no
force and effect until amended to comply with Code Section&nbsp;409A (which
amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by the AJCA Guidance).



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;The Plan Administrator shall not take any action that would violate
any provision of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. It is intended that, to the extent
applicable, all Participant elections hereunder will comply with Code Section
409A and the AJCA Guidance. The Plan Administrator is authorized to adopt
rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in connection therewith to
anticipate and/or comply with the requirements thereof (including any
transition or grandfather rules thereunder). In this regard, the Plan
Administrator is authorized to permit Participant elections with respect to
amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 and is also permitted to allow the
Participants the right to amend or revoke such elections in accordance with the
AJCA Guidance.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;6 to this Plan is January&nbsp;1, 2005.
This Amendment creates additional Sub-Accounts (where necessary) (i)&nbsp;to
reflect amounts that are &#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the AJCA
Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (collectively, the
&#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148;) and (ii)&nbsp;to reflect amounts that are deferred
after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Accounts&#148;).
Amendment No.&nbsp;6 also modifies the distribution elections and provisions for the
Post-2004 Sub-Accounts to comply with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;In furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing, any Excess
Retirement Benefit that is deemed to have been deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 and that qualifies for &#147;grandfathered status&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code shall continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified
deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code and
shall be subject to the terms and conditions specified in the Plan as in effect
prior to the effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;6. In particular, to the extent
permitted under AJCA Guidance:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and
Excess Matching Sub-Account as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 shall be credited to the
Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts and shall be paid under the terms of
the Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(ii)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess Profit Sharing Account as
of December&nbsp;31, 2004 including, to the extent permitted by the AJCA Guidance,
the Excess Profit Sharing Benefit for the 2004 Plan Year (which is allocated to
Participants&#146; Accounts in 2005), shall be credited to the Participant&#146;s
Grandfathered Sub-Account and shall be paid under the terms of the Plan as in
effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;2</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
sentences to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;In addition, the Sub-Accounts shall be further subdivided as follows:
(a)&nbsp;the Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account shall be divided into the Pre-2005
Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess Profit Sharing
Sub-Account; (b)&nbsp;the Excess 401(k) Sub-Account shall be divided into the
Pre-2005 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account
and (c)&nbsp;the Excess Matching Sub-Account shall be divided into the Pre-2005
Excess Matching Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess Matching Sub-Account. The
Pre-2005 Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account, the Pre-2005 Excess 401(k) Sub-


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">2
</DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Account and the Pre-2005 Excess Matching Sub-Account shall be referred to
herein collectively as the &#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148; and the remainder of
such Sub-Accounts shall be referred to herein as the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Accounts.&#148;



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;3</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.5 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentence to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the timing and crediting of Bonuses
hereunder shall be as specified in Section&nbsp;3.2.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;4</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.16 of the Plan is hereby amended by deleting the phrase &#147;Profit
Sharing Plan&#148; therein and replacing it with the phrase &#147;Profit Sharing
Retirement Plan.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;5</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.17 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;2.17 Unforeseeable Emergency shall mean an event which results in
a severe financial hardship to the Participant as a consequence of (a)&nbsp;an
illness or accident of the Participant, the Participant&#146;s spouse or a dependent
within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;152, (b)&nbsp;loss of the Participant&#146;s property
due to casualty or (c)&nbsp;other similar extraordinary and unforeseeable
circumstances arising as a result of events beyond the control of the
Participant.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;6</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;II of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
definitions to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;2.19 Bonus shall mean any bonus under any annual bonus plan that
would be taken into account as Compensation under the Profit Sharing Plan,
which is earned with respect to services performed by a Participant during a
Plan Year (whether or not such Bonus is actually paid to the Participant during
such Plan Year). An election to defer a Bonus under this Plan must be made
before the period in which the services are performed which gives rise to such
Bonus.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.20 Disability or Disabled. A Participant shall be deemed to
have a &#147;Disability&#148; or be &#147;Disabled&#148; if the Participant (a)&nbsp;is unable to engage
in any substantial gainful activity by reason of any medically determinable
physical or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or can
be expected to last for a continuous period of not less than twelve months, or
(b)&nbsp;is, by reason of any medically determinable physical or mental impairment
which can be expected to result in death or can be expected to last for a
continuous period of not less than twelve months, receiving income replacement
benefits for a period of not less than three months under an Employer-sponsored
accident and health plan.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.21 Key Employee shall mean a key employee, as defined in Section
416(i) of the Code (without regard to paragraph (5)&nbsp;thereof) of the Company (as
long as the stock of which is publicly traded on an established securities
market or otherwise).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.22 Termination of Employment means a separation of service as
defined in the AJCA Guidance issued under Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;7</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.2(a) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(a) Amount of Excess 401(k) Benefits. Each 401(k) Employee who is a
Participant may, within 30&nbsp;days after the Plan becomes effective as to him and
on or prior to each December&nbsp;31st thereafter, by completing an approved
deferral election form, direct the Company to reduce his Compensation for the
balance of the Plan Year in which the Plan becomes effective as to him (but
only with respect to Compensation payable for periods of service commencing
after the 401(k) Employee so directs) or for the Plan Year following any such
December&nbsp;31, respectively, by an amount equal to the difference between (i)&nbsp;a
specified percentage, in 1% increments, with a maximum of 25%, of his
Compensation for the Plan Year, and (ii)&nbsp;the maximum Before-Tax Contributions
actually permitted to be contributed for him to the Profit Sharing Plan for
such Plan Year by reason of the application of the limitations under Sections
402(g), 401(a)(17), 401(k)(3) and 414(v) of the Code. All amounts deferred
under this Section shall be referred to herein collectively as the &#147;Excess
401(k) Benefits.&#148; Notwithstanding the foregoing, a 401(k) Employee&#146;s direction
to reduce a Bonus earned during a particular Plan Year shall be made no later
than December&nbsp;31st of the Plan Year preceding the Plan Year in which the Bonus
commences to be earned (or, in the case of the first year in which a
Participant becomes eligible to participate in the Plan, within 30&nbsp;days after
the Plan becomes effective as to him) and, as a result, Bonuses that are paid
in 2005 shall not be taken into account for purposes of calculating Excess
401(k) Benefits hereunder.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;8</B>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, (1)&nbsp;distributions of Post-2004 Sub-Accounts
under the circumstances described in clauses (A)&nbsp;or (B)&nbsp;shall only be made in
the event of a Termination of Employment, (2)&nbsp;distributions of Post-2004
Sub-Accounts to Key Employees made on account of a Termination of Employment
may not be made before the date that is six months thereafter (or, if earlier,
the date of death) and (3)&nbsp;Participants may not elect a payment date that is
the &#147;later of&#148; the dates specified in clauses (A)&nbsp;through (E)&nbsp;above.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;9</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.4(a) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(iii) Notwithstanding the foregoing, Participants shall be required to
make an election of a payment date for their Post-2004 Sub-Accounts by December
31, 2004 (or, if later, prior to their initial participation) and such
elections shall be made in accordance with the requirements of Code Section
409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;10</B>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, a Participant must make a new deferral election
to participate in the Plan for the 2005 Plan Year.&#148;

Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts or the Post-2004 Sub-Accounts, as
applicable, in accordance with Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;

on Accounts under the Plan at any time upon at least 30&nbsp;days advance notice to

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;17</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1(b) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
clause (iv)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(iv) Clauses (ii)&nbsp;and (iii)&nbsp;above shall not apply to a Participant&#146;s
Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account or Post-2004 Excess Matching Sub-Account.
The Participant shall elect a form of payment for such Sub-Accounts prior to
December&nbsp;31, 2004 (or when the Plan first becomes applicable to him, if later).
He may elect to receive such Sub-Accounts in the form of a lump sum payment or
in the form of annual installment payments (for 10 or fewer years), with the
installment payments (if any) being calculated in accordance with the rules
specified in clause (ii). If the Participant does not make a timely election
regarding the form of payment, his Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and
Post-2004 Excess Matching Sub-Account shall be distributed in the form of a
single lump sum payment. Once made, the election (or deemed election) of a
form of payment under this clause (iv)&nbsp;shall be irrevocable except as specified
in the following sentences. Notwithstanding the foregoing, a Participant may
change his form of payment election (or deemed election) for his Post-2004
Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and Post-2004 Excess Matching Sub-Account by filing a
subsequent notice in writing, signed by the Participant and filed with the Plan
Administrator. However, unless otherwise permitted in accordance with Code
Section&nbsp;409A, such election will not be effective unless (A)&nbsp;it is made not
less than twelve months prior to the date that distribution would have been
made absent such election, (B)&nbsp;the first payment under such election will be
made no less than five years from the date payment would have been made absent
such election (excluding distributions made on account of the death of the
Participant), (C)&nbsp;such election will not take effect until at least twelve
months after the date on which the election is made and (D)&nbsp;the election does
not accelerate the form of payment.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;18</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The second sentence of Section&nbsp;7.1(c) of the Plan is hereby amended in its
entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Payments made on account of an Unforeseeable Emergency shall be permitted
only to the extent the amount does not exceed the amount reasonably necessary
to satisfy the emergency need (plus an amount necessary to pay taxes reasonably
anticipated as a result of the distribution) and may not be made to the extent
such Unforeseeable Emergency is or may be relieved through reimbursement or
compensation by insurance or otherwise or by liquidation of the Participant&#146;s
assets (to the extent such liquidation would not itself cause severe financial
hardship).&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;19</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1(e) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
sentence to the beginning thereof:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;The provisions of this Subsection (e)&nbsp;shall only apply to the amounts
that are allocated to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">6
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;20</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The last sentence of Section&nbsp;7.1(f) of the Plan is hereby amended in its
entirety, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;The Compensation Committee of the Board of Directors of the Company, in
its sole and absolute discretion, shall have the authority to waive this
payment restriction (in whole or in part) upon the written request of the
Participant, to the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;21</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
Subsection (g)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(g) Each of the foregoing provisions of this Section shall apply only to
the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;22</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;8.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
Subsection (d)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(d) Notwithstanding the foregoing, distributions to Beneficiaries of
amounts that are allocated to Participants&#146; Post-2004 Sub-Accounts shall be
made in a manner that satisfies the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;23</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first paragraph of Section&nbsp;10.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by
deleting the last sentence thereof.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;24</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of the third paragraph of Section&nbsp;10.3 of the Plan is
hereby amended in its entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;A claimant whose claim is denied (or his duly authorized representative) who
wants to contest that decision must file with the Plan Administrator a written
request for a review of such claim within 60&nbsp;days after receipt of denial of a
claim.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;25</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The fourth paragraph of Section&nbsp;10.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by
deleting the last sentence thereof.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;26</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;10.5 of the Plan is hereby amended by (i)&nbsp;deleting the phrase &#147;the
Committee&#148; from the first sentence thereof, and replacing it with the phrase,
&#147;the Company (with the approval or ratification of the Benefits Committee)&#148; and
(ii)&nbsp;deleting the word &#147;Committee&#148; from the second sentence thereof and
replacing it with the phrase &#147;Benefits Committee.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">7
</DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;27</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A new Section&nbsp;10.7 is hereby added to the end of the Plan, to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;10.7. The Company reserves the right to amend the Plan in any
respect, without the consent of any person, in order to comply with Code
Section&nbsp;409A. The provisions of Articles IX and X shall apply only to the
extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;

this 28th day of December, 2004.

<FILENAME>l11171aexv10w2.htm
<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #7 RETIREMENT BENEFIT PLAN FOR RANKIN

<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.2</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt"><B
>Exhibit 10.2</B>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 7<BR>
TO THE RETIREMENT BENEFIT PLAN<BR>
FOR ALFRED M. RANKIN, JR.<BR>
(As Amended and Restated Effective as of January&nbsp;1, 1994)</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, NACCO Industries, Inc. (the &#147;Employer&#148;) originally adopted the
Retirement Benefit Plan for Alfred M. Rankin Jr. (the &#147;Plan&#148;) effective as of
March&nbsp;1, 1989 and has since amended the Plan; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW THEREFORE, the Employer hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;7 to the
Plan, which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to
January&nbsp;1, 2005 to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and continue to be
governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to
the addition of Code Section&nbsp;409A (as specified in the Plan as in effect before
the adoption of this Amendment No.&nbsp;7) and (2)&nbsp;cause amounts deferred after
December&nbsp;31, 2004 to be deferred in compliance with the requirements of Code
Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words used herein with initial capital letters which are defined in the Plan
are used herein as so defined.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;I of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Section&nbsp;1.5 to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&#147;Section&nbsp;1.5. American Jobs Creation Act (AJCA).



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;It is intended that the Plan (including any Amendments thereto) comply
with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as enacted by the AJCA, so as
to prevent the inclusion in gross income of any amount credited to the
Participant&#146;s Account hereunder in a taxable year that is prior to the taxable
year or years in which such amounts would otherwise be actually distributed or
made available to the Participant. The Plan shall be administered in a manner
that will comply with Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, including proposed, temporary
or final regulations


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">or any other guidance issued by the Secretary of the Treasury and the Internal
Revenue Service with respect thereto (collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA
Guidance&#148;). Any Plan provision that would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code (including, without limitation, any provisions of this
Amendment No.&nbsp;6) shall have no force and effect until amended to comply with
Code Section&nbsp;409A (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted
by the AJCA Guidance).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;Neither the Compensation Committee of the Board of Directors of the
Employer (the &#147;Compensation Committee&#148;) nor the NACCO Industries, Inc. Benefits
Committee shall take any action hereunder that would violate any provision of
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. It is intended that the Participant&#146;s elections
hereunder for amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 will comply with Code
Section&nbsp;409A and the AJCA Guidance. The Compensation Committee is authorized
to adopt rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in connection
therewith to anticipate and/or comply with the requirements thereof (including
any transition or grandfather rules thereunder).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of this Amendment No.&nbsp;7 is January&nbsp;1, 2005. As
stated below, this Amendment creates two separate Sub-Accounts for the
Participant &#151; (i)&nbsp;the &#147;Grandfathered Sub-Account&#148; for amounts that are
&#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the AJCA Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31,
2004 (and earnings thereon) and (ii)&nbsp;the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts
that are deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon). This
Amendment also modifies the distribution elections for the Post-2004
Sub-Account to comply with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A. In
furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing, any Supplemental Benefit
(and the earnings thereon) that are deemed to have been deferred prior to
January&nbsp;1, 2005 and that qualify for &#147;grandfathered status&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A
of the Code shall continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified
deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code and
shall be subject to the terms and conditions specified in the Plan as in effect
prior to the effective date of this Amendment No.&nbsp;7. In particular, to the
extent permitted under AJCA Guidance, the provisions of the Plan as in effect
prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 shall govern the Supplemental Benefits that are earned
during 2004, but credited to the Participant&#146;s Account in 2005.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;2</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1(1) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
sentence to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&#147;The Participant&#146;s Account shall be further divided into the following two
Sub-Accounts: (a)&nbsp;the &#147;Grandfathered Sub-Account&#148; for amounts that are
&#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the AJCA Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31,
2004 (and earnings thereon) and (b)&nbsp;the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts
that are deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon).&#148;



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;3</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1(5)(b) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the phrase &#147;or
any successors thereto&#148; to the end thereof.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-2-
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;4</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1(11) of the Plan is hereby amended by deleting the phrase
&#147;NACCO Materials Handling Group, Inc. Profit Sharing Plan&#148; and replacing it
with the phrase &#147;NACCO Materials Handling Group, Inc. Profit Sharing Retirement
Plan&#148; therein.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;5</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1(16) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;SECTION 2.1(16). Unforeseeable Emergency shall mean an event which
results in severe financial hardship to the Participant as a consequence of (a)
an illness or accident of the Participant, the Participant&#146;s spouse or
dependent (within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;152(a)), (b)&nbsp;a loss of the
Participant&#146;s property due to casualty or (c)&nbsp;other similar extraordinary and
unforeseeable circumstances arising as a result of events out of the control of
the Participant.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;6</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new paragraph to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;The Employer shall make such credits and debits to the Participant&#146;s
Grandfathered Sub-Account or Post-2004 Sub-Account, as applicable.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;7</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.4(d) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(d) Changes in Earnings Assumptions. The Compensation Committee may
change the earnings rate credited on the Participant&#146;s Account hereunder, to
the extent permitted under Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;8</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.1 of the Plan is hereby amended (1)&nbsp;by renaming the Section as
&#147;Form and Timing of Distribution of Grandfathered Sub-Account&#148; and (2)&nbsp;by
adding the following new Subsection (g)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(g) Notwithstanding any provision of the Plan to the contrary, the rules
specified in this Section&nbsp;5.1 shall only apply (i)&nbsp;to the amounts allocated to
the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Account and (ii)&nbsp;to the extent that they do
not otherwise violate the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-3-
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;9</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;V of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
Section&nbsp;5.2 to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&#147;SECTION 5.2 Form and Timing of Distribution of Post-2004 Sub-Account.



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The provisions of this Section&nbsp;5.2 shall apply solely to distributions of
amounts that are allocated to a Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Sub-Account.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;Time of Payment. The Participant may irrevocably elect (at the time
specified, and otherwise in accordance with, the requirements of Code Section
409A) to receive the Supplemental Benefit that is allocable to his Post-2004
Sub-Account as soon as practicable following one of the following dates: (i)
the date on which he ceases to be employed by the Controlled Group, (ii)
January 1 of the year following the date on which he ceases to be employed by
the Controlled Group; (iii)&nbsp;the date on which he attains an age specified in
the election form; (iv)&nbsp;January 1 of the year following the date on which he
attains an age specified in the election form, or (v)&nbsp;the earlier or later of
any two such dates. Notwithstanding the foregoing, (1)&nbsp;distribution may not
commence until the Participant incurs a &#147;separation from service&#148; (as defined
in Code Section&nbsp;409A) and (2)&nbsp;if the Participant is a Key Employee (as defined
in Section 416(i) of the Code (without regard to paragraph (5)&nbsp;thereof)) of the
Employer, payment may not be made before the date that is 6&nbsp;months after the
date of such separation from service (or, if earlier, the date of death) to the
extent that Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B)(i) is applicable. If the Participant
does not make a timely election regarding the time of payment, his Supplemental
Benefit attributable to his Post-2004 Sub-Account shall be distributed to the
Participant in accordance with clause (i)&nbsp;of the first sentence of this
Subsection (subject to the limitations of the second sentence hereof). Once
made, the election (or deemed election) of a time of payment shall be
irrevocable.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;Form of Payment.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;The Participant may elect (at the time specified, and otherwise in
accordance with, the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A) to receive the
Supplemental Benefit that is allocable to his Post-2004 Sub-Account in the form
of a lump sum payment or in the form of annual installment payments (for 10
years or such other time period as elected by the Participant), with the
installment payments (if any) being calculated in accordance with the rules
specified in Section&nbsp;5.1. Any form of payment election must be in writing (on
a form provided by the Secretary of the Employer) and filed with the Secretary
of the Employer. If the Participant does not make a timely election regarding
the form of payment, his Supplemental Benefit attributable to his Post-2004
Sub-Account shall be distributed to the Executive in the form of a single lump
sum payment. Once made, the election (or deemed election) of a form of payment
under this Section&nbsp;5.2 shall be irrevocable except as specified in Section
5.2(b)(ii) below.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(ii)&nbsp;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Participant may change his form of
payment election (or deemed election) by filing a subsequent written election
with the Secretary of the Employer. However, such election will not be
effective unless (1)&nbsp;it is made not less than 12


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-4-
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">months prior to the date that distribution would have been made absent such
election, (2)&nbsp;the first payment under such election will be made no less than
five years from the date payment would have been made absent such election
(excluding distributions made on account of the death of the Participant), and
(3)&nbsp;such election will not take effect until at least 12&nbsp;months after the date
on which the election is made.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;Payment to Beneficiaries. In the event of the death of the
Participant, to the extent permitted under Code Section&nbsp;409A, his Beneficiary
shall receive a lump sum distribution of the balance of the Participant&#146;s
Post-2004 Sub-Account as soon as practicable after the Participant&#146;s death.
Notwithstanding the foregoing, to the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A,
the Participant may elect an alternate form of payment for his Beneficiary,
subject to the timing and other requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;Unforeseeable Emergency Distribution. Notwithstanding the foregoing,
the Employer may at any time, upon written request of the Participant, cause to
be paid to such Participant an amount equal to all or any part of the
Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Sub-Account if the Employer determines, based on such
reasonable evidence as it shall require, that such a payment or payments is
necessary for the purpose of alleviating the consequences of an Unforeseeable
Emergency. Payments made on account of an Unforeseeable Emergency shall be
permitted only to the extent the amount does not exceed the amount necessary to
satisfy the emergency need (plus amounts necessary to pay taxes reasonably
anticipated as a result of the distribution) and may not be made to the extent
such Unforeseeable Emergency is or may be relieved through reimbursement or
compensation by insurance or otherwise or by liquidation of the Participant&#146;s
assets (to the extent such liquidation would not itself cause severe financial
hardship.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;10</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;V of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Section&nbsp;5.3 to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;SECTION 5.3 Withholding/Taxes. To the extent required by applicable
law, the Employer shall withhold from the Supplemental Benefits hereunder any
income, employment or other taxes required to be withheld therefrom by any
federal, state or local government.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;11</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The second sentence of Section&nbsp;6.2 of the Plan is hereby deleted in its
entirety.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;12</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;6.4(a) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(a) The Employer shall be the sponsor of the Plan for purposes of ERISA.
The Compensation Committee shall be the Plan administrator and shall be
responsible for the general administration of the Plan and for carrying out the
provisions hereof. The Compensation


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-5-
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Committee shall have discretion to interpret the provisions of the Plan,
including, without limitation, by supplying omissions from, correcting
deficiencies in or in resolving inconsistencies or ambiguities in the language
of the Plan, to make factual findings with respect to any issue arising under
the Plan and to decide disputes arising under the Plan and to make any
determinations (including factual determinations) with respect to benefits
payable hereunder. Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Compensation Committee
shall not have the right to interpret the Plan in a manner that is inconsistent
with the requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;13</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;7.1 of the Plan is hereby amended in its
entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Subject to Section&nbsp;7.3, the Employer (with the approval or ratification
of the NACCO Industries, Inc. Benefits Committee) does hereby reserve the right
to amend, at any time, any or all of the provisions of the Plan, without the
consent of the Participant, Beneficiary or any other person.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;14</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.2 of the Plan is hereby amended by deleting the phrase
&#147;Committee&#148; and replacing it with the phrase &#147;Compensation Committee&#148; each time
it appears therein.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;15</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following clause
to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;; provided, however, that these limitations shall not apply to an
amendment or termination that the Company deems necessary to ensure compliance
with Section&nbsp;409A of the Code.&#148;

this 28<sup>th</SUP>&nbsp;day of December, 2004.

<TYPE>EX-10.3
<SEQUENCE>4
<FILENAME>l11171aexv10w3.htm
<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #1 N. AMERICAN COAL APPRECIATION PLAN
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.3</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 10.3</B>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 1<BR>
TO<BR>
THE NORTH AMERICAN COAL CORPORATION<BR>
VALUE APPRECIATION PLAN FOR YEARS 2000 TO 2009<BR>
WITH RESPECT TO<BR>
THE AMERICAN JOBS CREATION ACT OF 2004</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, The North American Coal Corporation (the &#147;Company&#148;) adopted The
North American Coal Corporation Value Appreciation Plan for Years 2000 to 2009
(the &#147;Plan&#148;) effective as of January&nbsp;1, 2000; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, to the fullest extent permitted by Section&nbsp;409A of the Code and
the AJCA Guidance, the Company wants to protect the &#147;grandfathered&#148; status of
VAP Awards that are deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW THEREFORE, the Company hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to the Plan,
which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and continue to be governed by the
law applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to the addition of
Section&nbsp;409A to the Code (as specified in the Plan as in effect prior to the
adoption of this Amendment No.&nbsp;1) and (2)&nbsp;cause amounts deferred after December
31, 2004 to be deferred in compliance with the requirements of Code Section
409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words used herein with initial capital letters that are defined in the Plan are
used herein as so defined.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;1 of the Plan is hereby amended by the addition of the following
new Section&nbsp;1A to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 1
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;1A <B>AMERICAN JOBS CREATION ACT (AJCA)</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;It is intended that the Plan (including any Amendments thereto) comply
with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as enacted by the AJCA, so as
to prevent the inclusion in gross income of any amount credited to a
Participant&#146;s VAP Account hereunder in a taxable year that is prior to the
taxable year or years in which such amounts would otherwise be actually
distributed or made available to the Participant. The Plan shall be
administered in a manner that will comply with Section&nbsp;409A of the Code,
including proposed, temporary or final regulations or any other guidance issued
by the Secretary of the Treasury and the Internal Revenue Service with respect
thereto (collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;). Any Plan provision
that would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A of the Code
(including any provision added by Amendment No.&nbsp;1 thereto) shall have no force
and effect until amended to comply with Code Section&nbsp;409A (which amendment may
be retroactive to the extent permitted by the AJCA Guidance).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;The Committee shall not take any action that would violate any
provision of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. The Committee is authorized to adopt
rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in connection with the
AJCA Guidance to anticipate and/or comply with the requirements thereof
(including any transition or grandfather rules thereunder).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to the Plan is January&nbsp;1, 2005.
Amendment No.&nbsp;1 creates two separate Sub-Accounts for each Participant&#146;s VAP
Account hereunder &#151; (i)&nbsp;the &#147;Pre-2005 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts that are
&#147;deferred&#148; (as such terms is defined in the AJCA Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31,
2004 (and earnings thereon) and (ii)&nbsp;the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts
that are deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;In furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing, any Award that
is deemed to have been deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 and that qualifies for
&#147;grandfathered status&#148; under
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code shall continue to be governed by the law applicable to
nonqualified deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the
Code and shall be subject to the terms and conditions specified in the Plan as
in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005. In particular, to the extent permitted
under the AJCA Guidance, all Awards that were issued (and, only if required
under the AJCA Guidance, vested) prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 shall be considered
&#147;grandfathered&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, shall be allocated to the
Participants&#146; Pre-2005 Sub-Account and shall be paid under the terms of the
Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;2</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Subsection (aa)&nbsp;to
the beginning thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(aa) &#147;Account&#148; means the account established in accordance with Section&nbsp;7
hereof to reflect the Participant&#146;s interest under the Plan. The Participant&#146;s
Account shall be further divided into the following two Sub-Accounts: (i)&nbsp;the
&#147;Pre-2005 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts that are &#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined
in the AJCA Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 2
</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">earnings thereon) and (ii)
the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Account&#148; for amounts that are deferred after December&nbsp;31,
2004 (and earnings thereon).&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;3</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2(b) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;4</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
definitions to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(q)&nbsp;&#147;Disability&#148; or &#147;Disabled.&#148; A Participant e shall be deemed to have a
&#147;Disability&#148; or be &#147;Disabled&#148; if the Participant (i)&nbsp;is unable to engage in any
substantial gainful activity by reason of any medically determinable physical
or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or can be
expected to last for a continuous period of not less than twelve months, or
(ii)&nbsp;is, by reason of any medically determinable physical or mental impairment
which can be expected to result in death or can be expected to last for a
continuous period of not less than twelve months, receiving income replacement
benefits for a period of not less than three months under an employer-sponsored
accident and health plan.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(r)&nbsp;&#147;Key Employee&#148; shall mean a key employee, as defined in Section
416(i) of the Code (without regard to paragraph (5)&nbsp;thereof) of the Company or
a Subsidiary (or related entity) so long as the Company or a related entity is
a corporation, any stock in which is publicly traded on an established
securities market or otherwise.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(s)&nbsp;&#147;Separation From Service&#148; means a separation of service as defined in
the AJCA Guidance issued under Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(t)&nbsp;&#147;Unforeseeable Emergency&#148; shall mean an event which results in a
severe financial hardship to the Participant as a consequence of (i)&nbsp;an illness
or accident of the Participant, the Participant&#146;s spouse or a dependent within
the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;152, (ii)&nbsp;loss of the Participant&#146;s property due to
casualty or (iii)&nbsp;other similar extraordinary and unforeseeable circumstances
arising as a result of events beyond the control of the Participant.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;5</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentence to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Committee shall not have the right to
take any action that would violate the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 3
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;6</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.2(a) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
paragraphs to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(aa) The payment provisions of paragraph (a)&nbsp;hereof shall only apply to
the payment of amounts that are allocated to a Participant&#146;s Pre-2005
Sub-Account. In addition, the Committee shall only be permitted to exercise
discretion with respect to the payment thereof to the extent that the exercise
of such discretion does not result in a &#147;material amendment&#148; of the Pre-2005
Sub-Account, determined in accordance with the AJCA Guidance.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(aaa)&nbsp;Subject to the provisions of Section&nbsp;5.2(f), the vested amounts in a
Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Sub-Account shall be payable as soon as practicable
following approval thereof by the Committee following the earliest to occur of
(1)&nbsp;December&nbsp;31, 2009 or (2)&nbsp;the date of a Participant&#146;s Separation from
Service for death, Disability or retirement (as defined above); provided,
however, in no event shall distribution be made with respect to a Key Employee
before the date that is six months after the date of Separation from Service of
the Key Employee (or, if earlier, the date of death), to the extent that Code
Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B)(i) is applicable.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;7</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;5.2(c) of the Plan is hereby amended in its
entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;As soon as practicable following Committee approval following the payment
dates specified above, the Company or Subsidiary shall deliver to the
Participant or, if applicable, his designated beneficiaries (or, if none, his
estate) a check in full payment of the amount represented by the Participant&#146;s
vested interest in his VAP Account.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;8</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.2(f) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentences to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, payments of amounts allocated to a
Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Sub-Account shall only be made on account of an
Unforeseeable Emergency and shall be permitted only to the extent the amount
does not exceed the amount reasonably necessary to satisfy the emergency need
(plus an amount necessary to pay taxes reasonably anticipated as a result of
the distribution) (or, if less, 40% of the Participant&#146;s vested interest in his
Post-2004 Sub-Account). Such payments may not be made to the extent such
Unforeseeable Emergency is or may be relieved through reimbursement or
compensation by insurance or otherwise or by liquidation of the Participant&#146;s
assets (to the extent such liquidation would not itself cause severe financial
hardship).&#148;

</DIV>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;; provided, however, that the Committee shall not take any action that

<TYPE>EX-10.4
