<FILENAME>l11171aexv10w4.htm
<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #5 N. AMERICAN COAL SUPPLEMENTAL RETIREMENT
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.4</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 10.4</B>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 5 AND INSTRUMENT OF BENEFIT FREEZE<BR>
TO THE NORTH AMERICAN COAL CORPORATION<BR>
SUPPLEMENTAL RETIREMENT BENEFIT PLAN<BR>
(As Amended and Restated effective September&nbsp;1, 1994)</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, The North American Coal Corporation (the &#147;Company&#148;) amended and
restated The North American Coal Corporation Supplemental Retirement Benefit
Plan (the &#147;Plan&#148;) effective September&nbsp;1, 1994 and has since amended the Plan;
and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, to the fullest extent permitted by Section&nbsp;409A of the Code and
the AJCA Guidance, the Company wants to protect the &#147;grandfathered&#148; status of
the Supplemental Retirement Benefits that are accrued prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005;
and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, due to the uncertainty regarding the affect of the AJCA on
Supplemental Retirement Benefits under the Plan, the Company has decided to
temporarily freeze all Supplemental Retirement Benefits as of December&nbsp;31,
2004;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW, THEREFORE, the Company hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;5 to the
Plan, which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to
January&nbsp;1, 2005 to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and continue to be
governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to
the addition of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code (as specified in the Plan as in effect
prior January&nbsp;1, 2005); and (2)&nbsp;temporarily freeze the accrual of Supplemental
Retirement Benefits hereunder as of December&nbsp;31, 2004.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words and phrases used herein with initial capital letters that are defined in
the Plan are used herein as so defined and the provisions hereof shall be
effective as of the close of business on December&nbsp;31, 2004.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;I of the Plan is hereby amended by the addition of the following
new Section&nbsp;1.6 at the end thereof to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;1.6 American Jobs Creation Act (AJCA).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;To the extent applicable, it is intended that the Plan (including all
Amendments thereto) comply with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as
enacted by the AJCA, so as to prevent the


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 1
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">inclusion in gross income of any
amount of Supplemental Retirement Benefit accrued hereunder in a taxable year
that is prior to the taxable year or years in which such amounts would
otherwise be actually distributed or made available to the Participants. The
Plan shall be administered in a manner that will comply with Section&nbsp;409A of
the Code, including proposed, temporary or final regulations or any other
guidance issued by the Secretary of the Treasury and the Internal Revenue
Service with respect thereto (collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;).
Any Plan provisions (including, without limitation, those added or amended by
Amendment No.&nbsp;5) that would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A of
the Code shall have no force and effect until amended to comply with Code
Section&nbsp;409A (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by the
AJCA Guidance).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;The Plan Administrator shall not take any action that would violate
any provision of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. The Plan Administrator is
authorized to adopt rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in
connection with the AJCA Guidance to anticipate and/or comply with the
requirements thereof (including any transition or grandfather rules
thereunder).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;5 to the Plan is December&nbsp;31,
2004. This Amendment temporarily freezes the Supplemental Retirement Benefits
under the Plan effective as of December&nbsp;31, 2004, with the intent being that
the Company will rescind the freeze upon issuance of the AJCA Guidance. In
furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing, any Supplemental Retirement
Benefit that is deemed to have been deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 and that
qualifies for &#147;grandfathered status&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the Code shall
continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred
compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code and shall be
subject to the terms and conditions specified in the Plan as in effect prior to
January&nbsp;1, 2005.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;2</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The fourth sentence of Section&nbsp;2.1(2)(B) of the Plan is hereby amended to
read as follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;The change of a Beneficiary under the Plan may be made, and may be
revoked, only by an instrument (in a form acceptable to the Company)
signed by the Participant and filed with the Plan Administrator prior to
the Participant&#146;s death.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;3</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1(10) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(10) &#147;Pension Plan&#148; shall mean The NACCO Industries, Inc. Pension
Plan for Salaried Employees (terminated November&nbsp;30, 1986), or Part&nbsp;I of
the Combined Defined Benefit Plan for NACCO Industries, Inc. and Its
Subsidiaries, which includes The NACCO Industries, Inc. Pension Plan for
Salaried Employees which was merged into such plan on December&nbsp;31, 1993)
(&#147;Plan 005&#148;). Pension accruals under Plan 005 for employees of NACCO
Industries, Inc. were generally frozen as of December&nbsp;31, 1993 and
pension accruals under Plan 005 for employees of all other Employers were
generally frozen as of December&nbsp;31, 2004; provided that such frozen
benefits are increased by a specified percentage for each year (in
accordance with the terms of Plan 005).&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 2
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;4</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;III of the Plan is hereby amended by the addition of the following
new Section&nbsp;3.2C thereto, immediately following Section&nbsp;3.2B, to read as
follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;3.2C Benefit Freeze. Notwithstanding any provision of the
Plan to the contrary, all Supplemental Retirement Benefits under the Plan
shall be frozen as of December&nbsp;31, 2004. In furtherance thereof, but
without limiting the foregoing, a Participant shall not receive credit
under this Plan for any service or compensation that is earned after
December&nbsp;31, 2004 (even if such service and compensation is taken into
account for purposes of calculating the Actual Pension Plan Benefit).
The Company intends that Supplemental Retirement Benefits that are
accrued (and, only if required under the AJCA Guidance, vested) on or
before December&nbsp;31, 2004 will qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status under
the AJCA and will continue to be governed by the law applicable to
nonqualified deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A
of the Code.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;5</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;4.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by the addition of the following
new sentence at the end thereof to read as follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, to the extent that the provisions of
Amendment No.&nbsp;7 to Plan 005 (i.e., the provision that fully vests all
Participants in their Pension Plan benefits as of December&nbsp;31, 2004)
would otherwise be deemed a &#147;material amendment&#148; under the AJCA Guidance
and cause Section&nbsp;409A of the Code to apply to &#147;grandfathered&#148; benefits
hereunder, such provisions of Amendment No.&nbsp;7 to Plan 005 shall not be
taken into account in determining a Participant&#146;s vested interest in his
Supplemental Retirement Plan Benefit hereunder.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;6</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.2 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
clause to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;and provided further that this provision shall not apply to the extent it
violates Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;7</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;5.4 of the Plan is hereby amended to read as
follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;Any member of the Controlled Group that has adopted a Pension Plan may
become an Employer hereunder with the written consent of the NACCO
Industries, Inc. Benefits Committee (the &#147;Benefits Committee&#148;) if it
executes an &#147;Instrument of Adoption&#148; evidencing its adoption of the Plan
and files a copy thereof with the Company.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 3
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;8</B>




<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.5(1) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(1)&nbsp;The Compensation Committee shall be responsible for the general
administration of the Plan and for carrying out the provisions hereof
and, for purposes of the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974,
as amended, the Company shall be the plan sponsor and the plan
administrator. The Compensation Committee shall interpret where
necessary, in its reasonable and good faith judgment, the provisions of
the Plan and, except as otherwise provided in the Plan, shall determine
the rights and status of Participants and Beneficiaries hereunder
(including, without limitation, the amount of any Supplemental Retirement
Benefit to which a Participant or Beneficiary may be entitled under the
Plan); provided, however, that the Compensation Committee shall not take
any action that violates Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;9</B>




<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.7 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;5.7 Claims Procedure.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(1) Any Participant or Beneficiary who believes that he is entitled
to receive a benefit under the Plan which he has not received may file
with the Compensation Committee a written claim specifying the basis for
his claim and the facts upon which he relies in making such a claim.
Such a claim must be signed by the claimant or his duly authorized
representative (the &#147;Claimant&#148;).



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(2) Whenever the Compensation Committee denies (in whole or in
part), a claim for benefits filed by a Claimant, the Compensation
Committee shall transmit a written notice of such decision to the
Claimant, within 90&nbsp;days after such claim was filed (plus an additional
period of 90&nbsp;days if required for processing, provided that notice of the
extension of time is given to the Claimant within the first 90&nbsp;day
period). Such notice shall be written in a manner calculated to be
understood by the Claimant and shall state (a)&nbsp;the specific reason(s) for
the denial of the claim, (b)&nbsp;specific reference(s) to pertinent
provisions of the Plan on which the denial of the claim was based, (c)&nbsp;a
description of any additional material or information necessary for the
Claimant to perfect the claim and an explanation of why such material or
information is necessary, and (d)&nbsp;an explanation of the Plan&#146;s review
procedures under Subsection (3)&nbsp;below and the time limits applicable to
such procedures, including a statement of the Claimant&#146;s right to bring a
civil action under Section 502(a) of ERISA following an adverse benefit
determination on review.



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(3) Within 60&nbsp;days after the denial of his claim, the Claimant must
request that the claim denial be reviewed by filing with the Compensation
Committee a written request therefor. If such an appeal is not filed
within this 60-day limit, the Claimant shall be deemed to have agreed
with the Compensation Committee&#146;s denial of the claim. If such an appeal
is so filed within such 60 days, a named fiduciary designated by the
Compensation Committee shall (a)&nbsp;conduct a full and fair review of such
claim and (b)&nbsp;mail or deliver to the Claimant a written decision on the
matter based on the facts and pertinent provisions of the Plan within a
period of 60&nbsp;days after the receipt of the request for review unless
special circumstances require an extension of time, in which case such
decision shall be rendered not later than 120&nbsp;days after receipt of such
request. If an extension of time for review is required, written notice
of the extension shall be furnished to the Claimant prior to the
commencement of the extension. Such decision (a)&nbsp;shall be written in a
manner calculated to be understood by the Claimant, (b)&nbsp;shall


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 4
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">state the specific reason(s) for the decision, (c)&nbsp;shall make specific
reference(s) to pertinent provisions of the Plan on which the decision is
based and (d)&nbsp;shall, to the extent permitted by applicable law, be final
and binding on all interested persons. During such full review, the
Claimant shall be given an opportunity to review documents that are
pertinent to the Claimant&#146;s claim and to submit issues and comments in
writing. In addition, the notice of adverse determination shall also
include statements that (a)&nbsp;the Claimant is entitled to receive, upon
request and free of charge, reasonable access to, and copies of, all
documents, records and other information relevant to the Claimant&#146;s claim
for benefits and (b)&nbsp;a statement of the Claimant&#146;s right to bring an
action under Section 502(a) of ERISA.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;10</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;6.1 of the Plan is hereby amended to read as
follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;Subject to Section&nbsp;6.3, the Company (with the approval or ratification
of the Benefits Committee) does hereby reserve the right to amend, at any
time, any or all of the provisions of the Plan for all Employers, without
the consent of any other Employer or any Participant, Beneficiary or any
other person.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;11</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;6.2(1) of the Plan is hereby amended to read
as follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;The Board of Directors of the Company (and/or the Compensation Committee
thereof) does hereby reserve the right to terminate the Plan at any time
for any or all Employers, without the consent of any other Employer or of
any Participant, Beneficiary or any other person.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;12</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;6.3(1) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
clause to the end thereof, to read as follows:



<P align="left" style="margin-left:3%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;provided, however, that such limitations shall not apply to the extent
deemed necessary by the Company to comply with the requirements of Code
Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 5
</DIV>

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Section&nbsp;6.3(2) of the Plan is hereby amended by
adding the following clause to the end thereof, read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;; to the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;EXECUTED this 28<sup>th</SUP>&nbsp;day of December, 2004.

<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #4 N. AMERICAN COAL COMP PLAN FOR MANAGEMENT
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.5</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 10.5</B>


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 4<BR>
TO THE NORTH AMERICAN COAL CORPORATION<BR>
DEFERRED COMPENSATION PLAN FOR MANAGEMENT EMPLOYEES<BR>
(As Amended and Restated Effective as of November&nbsp;1, 2001)<BR>
WITH RESPECT TO<BR>
THE AMERICAN JOBS CREATION ACT OF 2004</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, The North American Coal Corporation (the &#147;Company&#148;) adopted an
amended and restated Deferred Compensation Plan for Management Employees (the
&#147;Plan&#148;) effective as of November&nbsp;1, 2000 and has since amended the Plan; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued; and



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to Article&nbsp;V of the Plan, all amounts credited to a
Participant&#146;s Account under the Plan are 100% vested; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, to the fullest extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A and the AJCA
Guidance, the Company wants to protect the &#147;grandfathered&#148; status of the Excess
Retirement Benefits that were deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW THEREFORE, the Company hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;4 to the Plan,
which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 (including any earnings thereon) to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and
continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred
compensation, and the terms of the Plan as in effect, prior to the addition of
Code Section&nbsp;409A and (2)&nbsp;cause amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 to be
deferred in compliance with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words used herein with initial capital letters which are defined in the Plan
are used herein as so defined and the provisions hereof shall be effective
January&nbsp;1, 2005.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;I of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Section&nbsp;1.6 to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;1.6 American Jobs Creation Act (AJCA).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;It is intended that the Plan (including all Amendments thereto) comply
with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as enacted by AJCA, so as to
prevent the inclusion in gross income of any Excess Retirement Benefit
hereunder in a taxable year that is prior to the taxable year or years in which
such amounts would otherwise actually be distributed or made available to the
Participants. The Plan shall be administered in


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 1
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">a manner that will comply with
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, including any proposed, temporary or final
regulations or any other guidance issued by the Secretary of
the Treasury and the Internal Revenue Service with respect thereto
(collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;). Any Plan provisions
(including, without limitation, those added or amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;4) that
would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A of the Code shall have no
force and effect until amended to comply with Code Section&nbsp;409A (which
amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by the AJCA Guidance).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;The Plan Administrator shall not take any action that would violate
any provision of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. It is intended that, to the extent
applicable, all Participant elections hereunder will comply with Code Section
409A and the AJCA Guidance. The Plan Administrator is authorized to adopt
rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in connection therewith to
anticipate and/or comply with the requirements thereof (including any
transition or grandfather rules thereunder). In this regard, the Plan
Administrator is authorized to permit Participant elections with respect to
amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 and is also permitted to allow the
Participants the right to amend or revoke such elections in accordance with the
AJCA Guidance.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;4 to this Plan is January&nbsp;1, 2005.
This Amendment creates additional Sub-Accounts (where necessary) (i)&nbsp;to
reflect amounts that are &#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the AJCA
Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (collectively, the
&#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148;) and (ii)&nbsp;to reflect amounts that are deferred
after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Accounts&#148;).
Amendment No.&nbsp;4 also modifies the distribution elections and provisions for the
Post-2004 Sub-Accounts to comply with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;In furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing, any Excess
Retirement Benefit that is deemed to have been deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 and that qualifies for &#147;grandfathered status&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code shall continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified
deferred compensation prior to the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code and
shall be subject to the terms and conditions specified in the Plan as in effect
prior to the effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;4. In particular, to the extent
permitted under AJCA Guidance:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;No additional VAP Deferral Benefits are permitted under the Plan and,
as a result, the VAP Deferral Sub-Account shall be classified as a
Grandfathered Sub-Account and shall be paid under the terms of the Plan as in
effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(ii)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and
Excess Matching Sub-Account as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 shall be credited to the
Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts and shall be paid under the terms of
the Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(iii)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess Profit Sharing Account
as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 including, to the extent permitted by the AJCA
Guidance, the Excess Profit Sharing Benefit for the 2004 Plan Year (which is
allocated to Participants&#146; Accounts in 2005), shall be credited to the
Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Account and shall be paid under the terms of
the Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.&#148;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;24</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.3 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;SECTION 9.3. Claims and Appeals Procedures.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;The Plan Administrator shall determine the rights of any person to any
Excess Retirement Benefits hereunder. Any person who believes that he has not
received the Excess Retirement Benefits to which he is entitled under the Plan
must file a claim in writing with the Plan Administrator specifying the basis
for his claim and the facts upon which he relies in making such a claim. Such
a claim must be signed by the claimant or his duly authorized representative
(the &#147;Claimant&#148;).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;Whenever the Plan Administrator denies (in whole or in part) a claim
for benefits under the Plan, the Plan Administrator shall transmit a written
notice of such decision to the Claimant, no later than 90&nbsp;days after the
receipt of a claim (plus an additional period of 90&nbsp;days if required for
processing, provided that notice of the extension of time is given to the
claimant within the first 90&nbsp;day period). Such notice shall be written in a
manner calculated to be understood by the Claimant and shall state (i)&nbsp;the
specific reasons for the denial; (ii)&nbsp;specific reference to pertinent Plan
provisions on which the denial is based; (iii)&nbsp;a description of any additional
material or information necessary for the Claimant to perfect the claim and an
explanation of why such material or information is necessary; and (iv)&nbsp;an
explanation of the Plan&#146;s claim review procedure and the time limits applicable
thereto (including a statement of the
Claimant&#146;s right to bring a civil action under Section 502(a) of ERISA
following an adverse benefit determination on review).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;Within 60&nbsp;days after receipt of denial of a claim, the Claimant must
file with the Plan Administrator a written request for a review of such claim.
If such an appeal is not filed within such 60-day period, the Claimant shall be
deemed to have acquiesced in the original decision of the Plan Administrator on
his claim. If such an appeal is so filed within such 60&nbsp;day period, a named
fiduciary designated by the Plan Administrator shall conduct a full and fair
review of such claim. During such review, the Claimant shall be given the
opportunity to review documents that are pertinent to his claim and to submit
issues and comments in writing. For this purpose, the named fiduciary shall
have the same power to interpret the Plan and make findings of fact thereunder
as is given to the Plan Administrator under Section&nbsp;9.1 above. The named
fiduciary shall mail or deliver to the Claimant a written decision on the
matter based on the facts and the pertinent provisions of the Plan within 60
days after the receipt of the request for review (unless special circumstances
require an extension of up to 60 additional days, in which case written notice
of such extension shall be given to the Claimant prior to the commencement of
such extension). Such decision (i)&nbsp;shall be written in a manner calculated to
be understood by the Claimant, (ii)&nbsp;shall state the specific reasons for the
decision and the specific Plan provisions on which the decision was based and
(iii)&nbsp;shall, to the extent permitted by applicable law, be final and binding on
all interested persons. In addition, the notice of adverse determination shall
also include statements that the Claimant is entitled to receive, upon request
and free of charge, reasonable access to, and copies of all documents, records
and other information relevant to the Claimant&#146;s claim for benefits and a
statement of the Claimant&#146;s right to bring a civil action under Section 502(a)
of ERISA.&#148;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;26</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The second sentence of Section&nbsp;9.5 of the Plan is hereby amended by
deleting the phrase &#147;such Committee&#148; and replacing it with the phrase &#147;the
Benefits Committee&#148; therein.


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;27</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;9.6 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;SECTION 9.6. Termination.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;The Board of Directors of the Company (or the Compensation Committee),
in its sole discretion, may terminate this Plan at any time and for any reason
whatsoever, except that, subject to Subsection (b)&nbsp;hereof, (i)&nbsp;no such
termination may adversely affect any Participant&#146;s Excess Retirement Benefit as
of the date of such termination, and (ii)&nbsp;no such termination may suspend the
crediting of earnings on the balance of a Participant&#146;s Account, until the
entire balance of such Account has been distributed, in either case, without
the prior written consent of the affected Participant. Any such termination
shall be expressed in the form of a written instrument executed by an officer
of the Company on the order of the Board (or Compensation Committee, as
applicable). Subject to the foregoing provisions of this Subsection, such
termination shall become effective as of the date specified in such instrument
or, if no such date is specified, on the date of its execution. Written notice
of any termination shall be given to the Participants as soon as practicable
after the instrument is executed.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;Notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, to the extent
permitted under Code Section&nbsp;409A, in the event of a termination of the Plan,
the Company, in its sole and absolute discretion (but with the consent of the
Benefits Committee or the Compensation Committee), shall have the right to
change the time and form of distribution of Participants&#146; Excess Retirement
Benefits, including requiring that all amounts credited to Participant&#146;s
Accounts hereunder be immediately distributed in the form of a lump sum
payment.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;Any Employer (other than the Company) that adopts the Plan may elect
to withdraw from the Plan and such withdrawal shall constitute a termination of
the Plan as to such Employer; provided, however, that such terminating Employer
shall continue to be an Employer for the purposes hereof as to Participants or
Beneficiaries to whom it owes obligations hereunder. Such withdrawal and
termination shall be expressed in an instrument executed by the terminating
Employer on authority of its Board of Directors (or the applicable Committee
thereof) and filed with the Company, and shall become effective as of the date
designated in such instrument or, if no such date is specified, on the date of
its execution. Notwithstanding any other provision of the Plan, if an Employer
(other than the Company) ceases to be a member of the Controlled Group, to the
extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A, the Plan shall automatically terminate
with respect to such Employer and all amounts credited to the Accounts of
Employees of such Employer shall be immediately payable in the form of a lump
sum payment.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;28</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A new Section&nbsp;9.7 is hereby added to the end of the Plan, to read as
follows:


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"> 8
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;9.7 AJCA. Notwithstanding any provision of the Plan to the
contrary, (a)&nbsp;the Company reserves the right to amend the Plan in any respect,
without the consent of any person, in order to comply with Code Section&nbsp;409A
and (b)&nbsp;the provisions of Article&nbsp;IX of the Plan shall apply only to the extent
permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;EXECUTED this 28<sup>th</SUP>&nbsp;day of December, 2004.

<TYPE>EX-10.6
<SEQUENCE>7
<FILENAME>l11171aexv10w6.htm
<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #9 NACCO MAT HAND UNFUNDED BENEFIT PLAN
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.6</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">
<P align="right" style="font-size: 10pt">Exhibit 10.6

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 9<BR>
TO<BR>
THE NACCO MATERIALS HANDLING GROUP, INC.<BR>
UNFUNDED BENEFIT PLAN<BR>
(As Amended and Restated Effective September&nbsp;1, 2000)<BR>
WITH RESPECT TO<BR>
THE AMERICAN JOBS CREATION ACT OF 2004</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, NACCO Materials Handling Group, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) adopted an
amended and restated Unfunded Benefit Plan (the &#147;Plan&#148;) effective as of
September&nbsp;1, 2000 and has since amended the Plan; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the Plan is classified as a &#147;nonqualified deferred compensation
plan&#148; under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004, P.L. 108-357 (the &#147;AJCA&#148;)
added a new Section&nbsp;409A to the Code, which significantly changed the Federal
tax law applicable to &#147;amounts deferred&#148; under the Plan after December&nbsp;31,
2004; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to the AJCA, the Secretary of the Treasury and the
Internal Revenue Service will issue proposed, temporary or final regulations
and/or other guidance with respect to the provisions of new Section&nbsp;409A of the
Code (collectively, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;); and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, the AJCA Guidance has not yet been issued; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, pursuant to Section&nbsp;6.1 of the Plan, all amounts credited to a
Participant&#146;s Account under the Plan are 100% vested; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS, to the fullest extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A and the AJCA
Guidance, the Company wants to protect the &#147;grandfathered&#148; status of the Excess
Retirement Benefits that were deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW THEREFORE, the Company hereby adopts this Amendment No.&nbsp;9 to the Plan,
which amendment is intended to (1)&nbsp;allow amounts deferred prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 (including any earnings thereon) to qualify for &#147;grandfathered&#148; status and
continue to be governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred
compensation, and the terms of the Plan as in effect, prior to the addition of
Code Section&nbsp;409A and (2)&nbsp;cause amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 to be
deferred in compliance with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Words used herein with initial capital letters that are defined in the Plan are
used herein as so defined.



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;1</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;I of the Plan is hereby amended by adding a new Section&nbsp;1.5 to the
end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;1.5 American Jobs Creation Act (AJCA).


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;It is intended that the Plan (including all Amendments thereto) comply
with the provisions of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code, as enacted by AJCA, so as to
prevent the inclusion in gross income of any Excess Retirement Benefit
hereunder in a taxable year that is prior to the taxable year or years in which
such amounts would otherwise actually be distributed or made available to the
Participants. The Plan shall be


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">1
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">administered in a manner that will comply with Section&nbsp;409A of the Code,
including any proposed, temporary or final regulations or any other guidance
issued by the Secretary of the Treasury and the Internal Revenue Service with
respect thereto (collectively with the AJCA, the &#147;AJCA Guidance&#148;). Any Plan
provisions (including, without limitation, those added or amended by Amendment
No.&nbsp;9) that would cause the Plan to fail to satisfy Section&nbsp;409A of the Code
shall have no force and effect until amended to comply with Code Section&nbsp;409A (which amendment may be retroactive to the extent permitted by the AJCA
Guidance).



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;The Plan Administrator shall not take any action that would violate
any provision of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. It is intended that, to the extent
applicable, all Participant elections hereunder will comply with Code Section
409A and the AJCA Guidance. The Plan Administrator is authorized to adopt
rules or regulations deemed necessary or appropriate in connection therewith to
anticipate and/or comply with the requirements thereof (including any
transition or grandfather rules thereunder). In this regard, the Plan
Administrator is authorized to permit Participant elections with respect to
amounts deferred after December&nbsp;31, 2004 and is also permitted to allow the
Participants the right to amend or revoke such elections in accordance with the
AJCA Guidance.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;The effective date of Amendment No.&nbsp;9 to this Plan is January&nbsp;1, 2005.
This Amendment creates additional Sub-Accounts (where necessary) (i)&nbsp;to
reflect amounts that are &#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the AJCA
Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (collectively, the
&#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148;) and (ii)&nbsp;to reflect amounts that are deferred
after December&nbsp;31, 2004 (and earnings thereon) (the &#147;Post-2004 Sub-Accounts&#148;).
Amendment No.&nbsp;9 also modifies the distribution elections and provisions for the
Post-2004 Sub-Accounts to comply with the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(d)&nbsp;In furtherance of, but without limiting the foregoing and except as
otherwise specifically provided herein, any Excess Retirement Benefit that is
deemed to have been deferred prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 and that qualifies for
&#147;grandfathered status&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the Code shall continue to be
governed by the law applicable to nonqualified deferred compensation prior to
the addition of Section&nbsp;409A to the Code and shall be subject to the terms and
conditions specified in the Plan as in effect prior to the effective date of
Amendment No.&nbsp;9. In particular, to the extent permitted under AJCA Guidance:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;The Excess Deferral Sub-Account and the Yale Short-Term Sub-Account
shall be allocated to the Grandfathered Sub-Accounts and shall be paid under
the terms of the Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(ii)&nbsp;On and after January&nbsp;1, 2005, the LTIP Deferral Sub-Account shall
only accept the deferral of LTIP Awards that (A)&nbsp;are 100% vested as of December
31, 2004, (B)&nbsp;with Grant Dates of January&nbsp;1, 2001, January&nbsp;1, 2002, January&nbsp;1,
2003 and January&nbsp;1, 2004 and (C)&nbsp;are validly and timely deferred under the LTIP
Plan and, as such, the LTIP Deferral Sub-Account shall be a Grandfathered
Sub-Account and shall be paid under the terms of the Plan as in effect prior to
January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(iii)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and
Excess Matching Sub-Account as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 shall be credited to the
Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts and shall be paid under the terms of
the Plan as in effect prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005; and


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(iv)&nbsp;Amounts allocated to a Participant&#146;s Excess Profit Sharing Account as
of December&nbsp;31, 2004 including, to the extent permitted by the AJCA Guidance,
the Excess Profit Sharing Benefit for the 2004 Plan Year (which is allocated to
the Participants&#146; Accounts in 2005), shall be credited to Participant&#146;s
Grandfathered Sub-Account.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">2
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;2</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
sentences to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;In addition, the Sub-Accounts shall be further subdivided as follows: (a)
the Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account shall be divided into the Pre-2005 Excess
Profit Sharing Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account;
(b)&nbsp;the Excess 401(k) Sub-Account shall be divided into the Pre-2005 Excess
401(k) Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and (c)&nbsp;the
Excess Matching Sub-Account shall be divided into the Pre-2005 Excess Matching
Sub-Account and the Post-2004 Excess Matching Sub-Account. The Pre-2005 Excess
Profit Sharing Sub-Account, the Pre-2005 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account, the
Pre-2005 Excess Matching Sub-Account, the Excess Deferral Sub-Account, the LTIP
Deferral Sub-Account and the Yale Short-Term Deferral Sub-Account shall be
referred to herein collectively as the &#147;Grandfathered Sub-Accounts&#148; and the
remainder of such Sub-Accounts shall be referred to herein as the &#147;Post-2004
Sub-Accounts.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;3</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.5 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentence to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the timing and crediting of Bonuses
hereunder shall be as specified in Section&nbsp;3.3.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;4</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.6 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;2.6 Employer shall mean the Company and NMHG Oregon, Inc.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;5</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.12(d) of the Plan is hereby amended by deleting the phrase &#147;or a
citizen or resident of the United Kingdom (referred to herein as &#147;UK
Participants&#148;), Brazil, Italy or Mexico&#148; therefrom.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;6</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.19 of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;2.19 Unforeseeable Emergency shall mean an event which results in
a severe financial hardship to the Participant as a consequence of (a)&nbsp;an
illness or accident of the Participant, the Participant&#146;s spouse or a dependent
within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;152, (b)&nbsp;loss of the Participant&#146;s property
due to casualty or (c)&nbsp;other similar extraordinary and unforeseeable
circumstances arising as a result of events beyond the control of the
Participant.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;7</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Article&nbsp;II of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
definitions to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;2.22 Bonus shall mean any bonus under the NACCO Materials
Handling Group, Inc. Annual Incentive Compensation Plan that would be taken
into account as Compensation under the Profit Sharing Plan, which is earned
with respect to services performed by a Participant during a Plan Year


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">3
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">(whether or not such Bonus is actually paid to the Participant during such Plan
Year). An election to defer a Bonus under this Plan must be made before the
period in which the services are performed which gives rise to such Bonus.



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.23 Key Employee shall mean a key employee, as defined in
Section 416(i) of the Code (without regard to paragraph (5)&nbsp;thereof) of an
Employer so long as the Company (or a related entity) is a corporation, any
stock in which is publicly traded on an established securities market or
otherwise.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.24 Termination of Employment means a separation of service as
defined in the AJCA Guidance issued under Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;8</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.2(b) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentence to the end thereof to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, no additional Post-1999 Excess Deferrals
shall be permitted to be made under the Plan.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;9</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.3(a) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to the end
thereof to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(a) Amount of Excess 401(k) Benefits. Each 401(k) Employee who is a
Participant may, within 30&nbsp;days after the Plan becomes effective as to him and
on or prior to each December&nbsp;31st thereafter, by completing an approved
deferral election form, direct his Employer to reduce his Compensation for the
balance of the Plan Year in which the Plan becomes effective as to him (but
only with respect to Compensation payable for periods of service commencing
after the 401(k) Employee so directs) or for the Plan Year following any such
December&nbsp;31, respectively, by an amount equal to the difference between (i)&nbsp;a
specified percentage, in 1% increments, with a maximum of 25%, of his
Compensation for the Plan Year, and (ii)&nbsp;the maximum Before-Tax Contributions
actually permitted to be contributed for him to the Profit Sharing Plan for
such Plan Year by reason of the application of the limitations under Sections
402(g), 401(a)(17), 401(k)(3) and 414(v) of the Code. All amounts deferred
under this Section shall be referred to herein collectively as the &#147;Excess
401(k) Benefits.&#148; Notwithstanding the foregoing, a 401(k) Employee&#146;s direction
to reduce a Bonus earned during a particular Plan Year shall be made no later
than December&nbsp;31st of the Plan Year preceding the Plan Year in which the Bonus
commences to be earned (or, in the case of the first year in which a
Participant becomes eligible to participate in the Plan, within 30&nbsp;days after
the Plan becomes effective as to him) and, as a result, Bonuses that are paid
in 2005 shall not be taken into account for purposes of calculating Excess
401(k) Benefits hereunder.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;10</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.5 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
Subsection (c)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(c) Notwithstanding the foregoing, the only LTIP Deferral Benefits that
shall be accepted hereunder are those with a Grant Date prior to January&nbsp;1,
2005 that are deemed to have been &#147;deferred&#148; (as such term is defined in the
AJCA Guidance) as of December&nbsp;31, 2004 and that qualify for grandfathered
status under the Act.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">4
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;11</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.7(a)(i) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
new sentence to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the payment date for amounts that are
allocated to the Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account of a Participant who has not
made a payment date election by December&nbsp;1, 2004 shall be the date on which he
incurs a Termination of Employment; provided, however, that (A)&nbsp;payment of
Excess Profit Sharing Benefits shall not occur until the date on which all
amounts allocable to the Participant&#146;s Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account for
the year of termination of employment have been credited to such Sub-Account
and (B)&nbsp;with respect to Key Employees, such payment may not be made before the
date which is six months after the date of the Key Employee&#146;s Termination of
Employment (or, if earlier, the date of death), to the extent that Code Section
409A(a)(2)(B)(i) is applicable.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;12</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.7(a)(ii) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read
as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(ii) Available Payment Dates. The Participant may elect to commence
payment of the Excess Deferral Sub-Account, the Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and
the LTIP Deferral Sub-Account, with separate elections being made for each such
Sub-Account as soon as practicable following (A)&nbsp;the date on which he ceases to
be an Employee of the Controlled Group, (B)&nbsp;the date on which he attains an age
specified in the deferral/payment election form or (C)&nbsp;the earlier or later of
such dates. Notwithstanding the foregoing, (X)&nbsp;payment of the Participant&#146;s
Excess Matching Sub-Account shall be made at the same time as the payment of
the Participant&#146;s Excess 401(k) Sub-Account and (Y)&nbsp;a Participant who does not
timely and properly file such an election form shall be deemed to have elected
to receive his Excess Deferral, Excess 401(k), Excess Matching, and LTIP
Deferral Sub-Accounts as soon as practicable following the date on which the
Participant ceases to be an Employee of the Controlled Group. In addition,
with respect to amounts that are allocated to a Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Excess
401(k) Sub-Account, (1)&nbsp;the Participant may only elect to receive a
distribution on the date on which he incurs a Termination of Employment or the
date he attains a specified age (or the earlier of such dates) and (2)&nbsp;with
respect to a Key Employee, a distribution on account of Termination of
Employment may not be made before the date which is six months after the date
of the Key Employee&#146;s Termination of Employment (or, if earlier, the date of
death), to the extent that Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B)(i) is applicable.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;13</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The first sentence of Sections&nbsp;3.7(c)(i) and Section&nbsp;3.7(c)(ii) of the
Plan are each hereby amended by adding the following new clause to the
beginning thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;To the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;14</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.7(c)(iii) of the Plan is hereby amended in its entirety to read
as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(iii) To the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A, any Participant whose
eligibility to make Before-Tax Contributions to the Profit Sharing Plan has
been involuntarily suspended because he has taken a Hardship withdrawal from
such plan shall automatically not be eligible to defer Excess 401(k) Benefits
under this Plan for his period of suspension from the Profit Sharing Plan. As
a result, such a Participant&#146;s deferral election hereunder shall automatically
be suspended for such time period and shall automatically be


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">5
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">reinstated following the end of such suspension (unless otherwise changed in
accordance with the terms of the Plan).&#148;



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;15</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;4.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
Subsection (i)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(i) The Employers shall make the above-described credits and debits to
the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts or the Post-2004 Sub-Accounts, as
applicable, in accordance with Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;16</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;5.4(a) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
clause to the beginning thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;To the extent not prohibited by Code Section&nbsp;409A,.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;17</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1(a) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new
sentences to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Notwithstanding the foregoing, with respect to amounts allocated to a
Participant&#146;s Post-2004 Excess Profit Sharing Sub-Account, such Benefits shall
be paid at the time specified in Section&nbsp;3.7 and shall automatically be paid in
the form of a single lump sum payment.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;18</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1(b) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following
clause (v)&nbsp;to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(v) Clauses (ii)&nbsp;and (iii)&nbsp;above shall not apply to a Participant&#146;s
Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account. The Participant shall elect a form of
payment for his Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account prior to December&nbsp;31, 2004
(or when the Plan first becomes applicable to him, if later). He may elect to
receive such Sub-Account in the form of a lump sum payment or in the form of
annual installment payments (for 10 or fewer years), with the installment
payments (if any) being calculated in accordance with the rules specified in
clause (ii). If the Participant does not make a timely election regarding the
form of payment, his Post-2004 Excess 401(k) Sub-Account shall be distributed
in the form of a single lump sum payment. Once made, the election (or deemed
election) of a form of payment under this clause (v)&nbsp;shall be irrevocable.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;19</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The second sentence of Section&nbsp;7.1(d) of the Plan is hereby amended in its
entirety to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Payments made on account of an Unforeseeable Emergency shall be permitted
only to the extent the amount does not exceed the amount reasonably necessary
to satisfy the emergency need (plus an amount necessary to pay taxes reasonably
anticipated as a result of the distribution) and may not be made to the extent
such Unforeseeable Emergency is or may be relieved through reimbursement or
compensation by


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">6
</DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">insurance or otherwise or by liquidation of the Participant&#146;s assets (to the
extent such liquidation would not itself cause severe financial hardship).&#148;



<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;20</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1(f)(i) of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;The provisions of this Subsection (f)&nbsp;shall only apply to the amounts
that are allocated to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Sub-Accounts.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;21</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The last sentence of Section&nbsp;7.1(g) of the Plan is hereby amended by
adding the following new clause to the end thereof, to read as follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;; to the extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;22</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;7.1 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(h) Each of the foregoing provisions of this Section shall apply only to

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;23</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;8.3 of the Plan is hereby amended by adding the following new

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;(d) Notwithstanding the foregoing, distributions to Beneficiaries of
amounts that are allocated to Participants&#146; Post-2004 Sub-Accounts shall be
made in a manner that satisfies the requirements of Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Section&nbsp;24</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A new Section&nbsp;12.1 is hereby added to the end of the Plan, to read as
follows:


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;Section&nbsp;12.1. The Company reserves the right to amend the Plan in any
respect, without the consent of any person, in order to comply with Code
Section&nbsp;409A. The provisions of Articles IX, X and XI shall apply only to the
extent permitted by Code Section&nbsp;409A.&#148;

this 28th day of December, 2004.

<DESCRIPTION>AMEND #4 NACCO MAT HAND LONG TERM INCENTIVE

<HEAD>
<TITLE>Ex-10.7</TITLE>
